Chapter 32

Aaron makes a golden calf, which Israel worships—Moses serves as a mediator between God and rebellious Israel—Moses breaks the tablets of stone—The Levites slay about 3,000 rebels—Moses pleads and intercedes for the people.

1 And when the people saw that Moses [adelayed](#note1a) to come down out of the mount, the people gathered themselves together unto Aaron, and said unto him, Up, make us [bgods](#note1b), which shall [cgo](#note1c) before us; for as for this Moses, the man that brought us up out of the land of Egypt, we [dwot](#note1d) not what is become of him.

2 And Aaron said unto them, Break off the [agolden](#note2a) earrings, which are in the ears of your wives, of your sons, and of your daughters, and bring them unto me.

3 And all the people brake off the golden earrings which were in their ears, and brought them unto Aaron.

4 And he received them at their hand, and fashioned it with a graving tool, after he had made it a [amolten](#note4a) calf: and they said, [bThese](#note4b) be thy [cgods](#note4c), O Israel, which brought thee up out of the land of Egypt.

5 And when Aaron saw it, he built an altar before it; and Aaron made proclamation, and said, To morrow is a feast to the Lord.

6 And they rose up early on the morrow, and offered burnt offerings, and brought [apeace offerings](#note6a); and the [bpeople](#note6b) sat down to eat and to drink, and rose up to play.

7 ¶ And the Lord said unto Moses, Go, get thee down; for thy people, which thou broughtest out of the land of Egypt, have [acorrupted](#note7a) themselves:

8 They have [aturned](#note8a) aside [bquickly](#note8b) out of the way which I commanded them: they have made them a [cmolten](#note8c) calf, and have worshipped it, and have sacrificed thereunto, and said, These be thy gods, O Israel, which have brought thee up out of the land of Egypt.

9 And the Lord said unto Moses, I have seen this people, and, behold, it is a [astiffnecked](#note9a) people:

10 Now therefore let me alone, that my [awrath](#note10a) may wax hot against them, and that I may [bconsume](#note10b) them: and I will make of thee a great [cnation](#note10c).

11 And Moses [abesought](#note11a) the Lord his God, and said, Lord, why doth thy wrath wax hot against thy people, which thou hast brought forth out of the land of Egypt with great power, and with a mighty hand?

12 Wherefore should the [aEgyptians](#note12a) speak, and say, For mischief did he bring them out, to slay them in the mountains, and to consume them from the face of the earth? Turn from thy fierce [bwrath](#note12b), and [crepent](#note12c) of this evil against thy people.

13 Remember [aAbraham](#note13a), Isaac, and Israel, thy servants, to whom thou [bswarest](#note13b) by thine own self, and saidst unto them, I will [cmultiply](#note13c) your [dseed](#note13d) as the stars of heaven, and all this [eland](#note13e) that I have spoken of will I give unto your seed, and they shall inherit it for ever.

14 [aAnd](#note14a) the Lord [brepented](#note14b) of the evil which he thought to do unto his people.

15 ¶ And Moses turned, and went down from the mount, and the two [atables](#note15a) of the testimony were in his hand: the tables were written on both their sides; on the one side and on the other were they written.

16 And the [atables](#note16a) were the work of God, and the [bwriting](#note16b) was the writing of God, graven upon the tables.

17 And when [aJoshua](#note17a) heard the noise of the people as they [bshouted](#note17b), he said unto Moses, There is a noise of war in the camp.

18 And he said, It is not the voice of them that [ashout for mastery](#note18a), neither is it the voice of them that cry for being overcome: but the noise of them that sing do I hear.

19 ¶ And it came to pass, as soon as he came nigh unto the camp, that he [asaw](#note19a) the calf, and the dancing: and Moses’ [banger](#note19b) waxed hot, and he cast the tables out of his hands, and [cbrake](#note19c) them beneath the mount.

20 And he took the [acalf](#note20a) which they had made, and burnt it in the fire, and ground it to powder, and [bstrawed](#note20b) it upon the [cwater](#note20c), and made the children of Israel drink of it.

21 And Moses said unto Aaron, What did this people unto thee, that thou hast brought so great a sin upon them?

22 And Aaron said, Let not the [aanger](#note22a) of my lord wax hot: thou knowest the people, that they are [bset](#note22b) on [cmischief](#note22c).

23 For they said unto me, [aMake](#note23a) us [bgods](#note23b), which shall go before us: for as for this Moses, the man that brought us up out of the land of Egypt, we wot not what is become of him.

24 And I said unto them, Whosoever hath any gold, let them break it off. So they gave it me: then I cast it into the fire, and there came out this calf.

25 ¶ And when Moses saw that the people were [anaked](#note25a); (for Aaron had made them [bnaked](#note25b) unto their shame among their enemies:)

26 Then Moses stood in the gate of the camp, and said, Who is on the Lord’s side? let him come unto me. And all the sons of Levi gathered themselves together unto him.

27 And he said unto them, Thus saith the Lord God of Israel, Put every man his sword by his side, and go in and out from gate to gate throughout the camp, and [aslay](#note27a) every man his brother, and every man his companion, and every man his neighbour.

28 And the children of Levi did according to the word of Moses: and there fell of the people that day about three thousand men.

29 For Moses had said, [aConsecrate](#note29a) yourselves to day to the Lord, even every man upon his [bson](#note29b), and upon his brother; that he may bestow upon you a [cblessing](#note29c) this day.

30 ¶ And it came to pass on the morrow, that Moses said unto the people, Ye have [asinned](#note30a) a great sin: and now I will go up unto the Lord; [bperadventure](#note30b) I shall make an [catonement](#note30c) for your sin.

31 And Moses returned unto the Lord, and said, Oh, this people have sinned a great sin, and have made them [agods](#note31a) of gold.

32 Yet now, if thou wilt [aforgive](#note32a) their sin—; and if not, [bblot](#note32b) me, I pray thee, out of thy [cbook](#note32c) which thou hast [dwritten](#note32d).

33 And the Lord said unto Moses, [aWhosoever](#note33a) hath [bsinned](#note33b) against me, him will I [cblot out](#note33c) of my [dbook](#note33d).

34 Therefore now go, [alead](#note34a) the people unto the place of which I have spoken unto thee: behold, mine [bAngel](#note34b) shall go before thee: nevertheless in the day when I visit I will visit their sin upon them.

35 And the Lord plagued the people, because they made the calf, which Aaron made.

Chapter 33

The Lord promises to be with Israel and drive out the people of the land—The tabernacle of the congregation is moved away from the camp—The Lord speaks to Moses face to face in the tabernacle—Later, Moses sees the glory of God but not His face.

1 And the Lord said unto Moses, [aDepart](#note1a), and go up hence, thou and the people which thou hast brought up out of the land of Egypt, unto the land which I sware unto Abraham, to Isaac, and to Jacob, saying, Unto thy [bseed](#note1b) will I give it:

2 And I will send an [aangel](#note2a) before thee; and I will drive out the [bCanaanite](#note2b), the Amorite, and the Hittite, and the Perizzite, the Hivite, and the Jebusite:

3 Unto a land [aflowing](#note3a) with milk and honey: for I will not go up in the midst of thee; for thou art a stiffnecked people: lest I consume thee in the way.

4 ¶ And when the people heard these evil tidings, they [amourned](#note4a): and no man did put on him his [bornaments](#note4b).

5 For the Lord had said unto Moses, Say unto the children of Israel, Ye are a [astiffnecked](#note5a) people: [bI](#note5b) will come up into the midst of thee in a moment, and consume thee: therefore now put off thy ornaments from thee, that I may know what to do unto thee.

6 And the children of Israel stripped themselves of their ornaments by the mount Horeb.

7 And Moses took the tabernacle, and pitched it without the camp, afar off from the camp, and called it the [aTabernacle](#note7a) of the congregation. And it came to pass, that every one which sought the Lord went out unto the [btabernacle of the congregation](#note7b), which was without the camp.

8 And it came to pass, when Moses went out unto the tabernacle, that all the people rose up, and stood every man at his [atent](#note8a) door, and looked after Moses, until he was gone into the tabernacle.

9 And it came to pass, as Moses entered into the tabernacle, the [acloudy pillar](#note9a) descended, and stood at the door of the tabernacle, and the Lord talked with Moses.

10 And all the people saw the cloudy pillar stand at the tabernacle door: and all the people rose up and worshipped, every man in his tent door.

11 And the Lord [aspake](#note11a) unto Moses [bface to face](#note11b), as a man [cspeaketh](#note11c) unto his [dfriend](#note11d). And he turned again into the camp: but his servant [eJoshua](#note11e), the son of [fNun](#note11f), a young man, departed not out of the tabernacle.

12 ¶ And Moses said unto the Lord, See, thou sayest unto me, [aBring](#note12a) up this people: and thou hast not let me know whom thou wilt send with me. Yet thou hast said, I [bknow](#note12b) thee by [cname](#note12c), and thou hast also found grace in my sight.

13 Now therefore, I pray thee, if I have found [agrace](#note13a) in thy sight, [bshew](#note13b) me now thy [cway](#note13c), that I may know thee, that I may find grace in thy sight: and consider that this nation is [dthy](#note13d) [epeople](#note13e).

14 And he said, My [apresence](#note14a) shall go with thee, and I will give thee [brest](#note14b).

15 And he said unto him, If thy presence go not with me, carry us not up hence.

16 For wherein shall it be known here that I and thy people have found grace in thy sight? is it not in that thou [agoest](#note16a) with us? so shall we be [bseparated](#note16b), I and thy people, from all the people that are upon the face of the earth.

17 And the Lord said unto Moses, [aI](#note17a) will [bdo](#note17b) this thing also that thou hast spoken: for thou hast found grace in my sight, and I know thee by name.

18 And he said, I beseech thee, [ashew](#note18a) me thy [bglory](#note18b).

19 And he said, I will make all my [agoodness](#note19a) pass before thee, and I will [bproclaim](#note19b) the name of the Lord before thee; and will be gracious to whom I will be gracious, and will shew [cmercy](#note19c) on whom I will shew mercy.

20 [aAnd](#note20a) he said, Thou canst not see my face: for [bthere](#note20b) shall no man [csee](#note20c) me, and live.

21 And the Lord said, Behold, there is a place by me, and thou shalt stand upon a rock:

22 And it shall come to pass, while my glory passeth by, that I will put thee in a clift of the rock, and will cover thee with my hand [awhile I pass by](#note22a):

23 And I will take away mine hand, and thou shalt [asee](#note23a) my [bback](#note23b) parts: but my face shall not be [cseen](#note23c).

Chapter 34

Moses hews new tables of stone—He goes up into Mount Sinai for forty days—The Lord proclaims His name and attributes and reveals His law—He makes another covenant with Israel—The skin of Moses’ face shines, and he wears a veil.

1 [aAnd](#note1a) the Lord said unto Moses, [bHew](#note1b) thee two [ctables](#note1c) of stone like unto the first: and I will [dwrite](#note1d) upon these tables the words that were in the first tables, which thou [ebrakest](#note1e).

2 And be ready in the morning, and come up in the morning unto mount Sinai, and present thyself there to me in the [atop](#note2a) of the mount.

3 And no man shall [acome](#note3a) up with thee, neither let any man be seen throughout all the mount; neither let the flocks nor herds feed before that mount.

4 ¶ And he hewed two [atables](#note4a) of stone like unto the first; and Moses rose up early in the morning, and went up unto mount Sinai, as the Lord had commanded him, and took in his hand the two tables of stone.

5 And the Lord descended in the cloud, and stood with him there, and [aproclaimed](#note5a) the name of the Lord.

6 And the Lord passed by before him, and proclaimed, The Lord, The Lord God, [amerciful](#note6a) and [bgracious](#note6b), [clongsuffering](#note6c), and abundant in [dgoodness](#note6d) and truth,

7 Keeping mercy for thousands, [aforgiving](#note7a) iniquity and transgression and [bsin](#note7b), [cand that](#note7c) will by no means [dclear](#note7d) the [eguilty](#note7e); visiting the [finiquity](#note7f) of the fathers upon the children, and upon the children’s children, unto the third and to the fourth generation.

8 And Moses made haste, and [abowed](#note8a) his head toward the earth, and worshipped.

9 And he said, If now I have found [agrace](#note9a) in thy sight, O Lord, let my Lord, I pray thee, go among us; for it is a [bstiffnecked](#note9b) people; and [cpardon](#note9c) our iniquity and our sin, and take us for [dthine](#note9d) [einheritance](#note9e).

10 ¶ And he said, Behold, I make a covenant: before all thy people I will do [amarvels](#note10a), such as have not been done in all the earth, nor in any nation: and all the people among which thou art shall see the work of the Lord: for it is a [bterrible](#note10b) thing that I will do with thee.

11 [aObserve](#note11a) thou that which I command thee this day: behold, I [bdrive](#note11b) out before thee the Amorite, and the Canaanite, and the Hittite, and the Perizzite, and the Hivite, and the Jebusite.

12 Take heed to thyself, lest thou make a [acovenant](#note12a) with the [binhabitants](#note12b) of the land whither thou goest, lest it [cbe for a](#note12c) snare in the midst of thee:

13 But ye shall [adestroy](#note13a) their [baltars](#note13b), break their images, and cut down their [cgroves](#note13c):

14 For thou shalt worship [ano](#note14a) other [bgod](#note14b): for the Lord, whose name is [cJealous](#note14c), is a [djealous](#note14d) God:

15 Lest thou make a [acovenant](#note15a) with the inhabitants of the land, and they go a [bwhoring](#note15b) after their [cgods](#note15c), and do sacrifice unto their gods, and [done](#note15d) [ecall](#note15e) thee, and thou [feat](#note15f) of his sacrifice;

16 And thou [atake](#note16a) of their [bdaughters](#note16b) unto thy sons, and their daughters go a whoring after their gods, and make thy sons go a whoring after their gods.

17 Thou shalt make thee no molten [agods](#note17a).

18 ¶ The [afeast](#note18a) of [bunleavened](#note18b) bread shalt thou keep. Seven days thou shalt eat unleavened bread, as I commanded thee, in the [ctime](#note18c) of the month [dAbib](#note18d): for in the [emonth](#note18e) Abib thou camest out from Egypt.

19 All that [aopeneth](#note19a) the [bmatrix](#note19b) is mine; and every firstling among thy cattle, whether ox or sheep, that is male.

20 But the firstling of an ass thou shalt redeem with a lamb: and if thou redeem him not, then shalt thou break his neck. All the [afirstborn](#note20a) of thy sons thou shalt redeem. And none shall appear before me empty.

21 ¶ Six days thou shalt work, but on the seventh day thou shalt [arest](#note21a): in [bearing](#note21b) time and in harvest thou shalt rest.

22 ¶ And thou shalt observe the [afeast](#note22a) of weeks, of the firstfruits of wheat harvest, and the feast of ingathering at the year’s end.

23 ¶ [aThrice](#note23a) in the year shall all your men children appear before the Lord God, the God of Israel.

24 For I will [acast out](#note24a) the nations before thee, and enlarge thy borders: neither shall any man [bdesire](#note24b) thy land, when thou shalt go up to appear before the Lord thy God thrice in the year.

25 Thou shalt not offer the [ablood](#note25a) of my sacrifice with [bleaven](#note25b); neither shall the sacrifice of the feast of the passover be [cleft](#note25c) unto the morning.

26 The first of the [afirstfruits](#note26a) of thy land thou shalt bring unto the house of the Lord thy God. Thou shalt not [bseethe](#note26b) a kid in his mother’s milk.

27 And the Lord said unto Moses, [aWrite](#note27a) thou these words: for [bafter](#note27b) the tenor of these words I have made a covenant with thee and with Israel.

28 And he was there with the Lord [aforty](#note28a) days and forty nights; he did neither [beat](#note28b) bread, nor drink water. And he [cwrote](#note28c) upon the tables the words of the [dcovenant](#note28d), the [eten](#note28e) [fcommandments](#note28f).

29 ¶ And it came to pass, when Moses came down from mount Sinai with the [atwo](#note29a) [btables](#note29b) of testimony in Moses’ hand, when he came down from the mount, that Moses [cwist](#note29c) not that the skin of his face [dshone](#note29d) while he talked with him.

30 And when Aaron and all the children of Israel saw Moses, behold, the skin of his face shone; and they were afraid to come nigh him.

31 And Moses called unto them; and Aaron and all the [arulers](#note31a) of the congregation returned unto him: and Moses talked with them.

32 And afterward all the children of Israel came nigh: and he gave them in commandment all that the Lord had spoken with him in mount Sinai.

33 And till Moses had done speaking with them, he put a [aveil](#note33a) on his face.

34 But when Moses went in before the Lord to speak with him, he took the veil off, until he came out. And he came out, and spake unto the children of Israel that which he was commanded.

35 And the children of Israel saw the face of Moses, that the skin of Moses’ face shone: and Moses put the veil upon his face again, until he went in to speak with him.

Chapter 35

Israel is admonished to observe the Sabbath—Free gifts are offered for the tabernacle—The calls and inspiration of certain artisans are confirmed.

1 And Moses gathered all the congregation of the children of Israel together, and said unto them, These are the words which the Lord hath commanded, that ye should do them.

2 [aSix](#note2a) days shall [bwork](#note2b) be done, but on the seventh day there shall be to you an holy day, a [csabbath](#note2c) of rest to the Lord: whosoever doeth work therein shall be put to [ddeath](#note2d).

3 Ye shall [akindle](#note3a) no fire throughout your habitations upon the sabbath day.

4 ¶ And Moses spake unto all the congregation of the children of Israel, saying, This is the thing which the Lord [acommanded](#note4a), saying,

5 Take ye from among you an offering unto the Lord: whosoever is of a [awilling](#note5a) heart, let him bring it, an offering of the Lord; gold, and silver, and brass,

6 And blue, and purple, and scarlet, and fine linen, and goats’ hair,

7 And rams’ skins dyed red, and badgers’ skins, and [ashittim](#note7a) wood,

8 And oil for the light, and spices for anointing oil, and for the sweet incense,

9 And onyx stones, and stones to be set for the [aephod](#note9a), and for the breastplate.

10 And [aevery wise hearted](#note10a) among you shall come, and make all that the Lord hath commanded;

11 The [atabernacle](#note11a), his tent, and his covering, [bhis taches](#note11b), and his boards, his bars, his pillars, and his sockets,

12 The [aark](#note12a), and the staves thereof, with the mercy seat, and the veil of the covering,

13 The [atable](#note13a), and his staves, and all [bhis vessels](#note13b), and the [cshewbread](#note13c),

14 The [acandlestick](#note14a) also for the light, and his furniture, and his lamps, with the [boil](#note14b) for the light,

15 And the [aincense](#note15a) altar, and his staves, and the [banointing oil](#note15b), and the sweet incense, and the [changing](#note15c) for the door at the entering in of the tabernacle,

16 The [aaltar](#note16a) of burnt offering, with his brasen grate, his staves, and all his vessels, the laver and [bhis foot](#note16b),

17 The hangings of the court, his pillars, and their sockets, and the hanging for the door of the court,

18 The [apins](#note18a) of the tabernacle, and the pins of the court, and their cords,

19 The [acloths of service](#note19a), to do service in the holy place, the holy garments for Aaron the priest, and the garments of his sons, to minister in the priest’s office.

20 ¶ And all the congregation of the children of Israel departed from the presence of Moses.

21 And they came, every one whose [aheart](#note21a) stirred him up, and every one whom his spirit made [bwilling](#note21b), and they brought the Lord’s [coffering](#note21c) [dto](#note21d) the work of the [etabernacle of the congregation](#note21e), and for all his service, and for the holy garments.

22 And they came, both men and women, as many as were willing hearted, and brought [abracelets](#note22a), and earrings, and rings, and tablets, all [bjewels of gold](#note22b): and every man that offered offered an [coffering](#note22c) of gold unto the Lord.

23 And every man, with whom was found blue, and purple, and scarlet, and fine [alinen](#note23a), and goats’ hair, and red skins of rams, and badgers’ skins, brought them.

24 Every one that did offer an offering of silver and brass brought the Lord’s [aoffering](#note24a): and every man, with whom was found shittim wood for any work of the service, brought it.

25 And all the women that were [awise](#note25a) hearted did spin with their hands, and brought that which they had spun, both of blue, and of purple, and of scarlet, and of fine linen.

26 And all the women whose heart stirred them up [ain wisdom](#note26a) spun goats’ hair.

27 And the [arulers](#note27a) brought onyx stones, and stones to be set, for the ephod, and for the breastplate;

28 And [aspice](#note28a), and oil for the light, and for the anointing oil, and for the sweet incense.

29 The children of Israel brought a [awilling](#note29a) offering unto the Lord, every man and woman, whose heart made them willing to bring for all manner of work, which the Lord had commanded to be made by the hand of Moses.

30 ¶ And Moses said unto the children of Israel, See, the Lord hath called by name [aBezaleel](#note30a) the son of Uri, the son of Hur, of the tribe of Judah;

31 And he hath filled him with the spirit of God, in [awisdom](#note31a), in understanding, and in knowledge, and in all manner of [bworkmanship](#note31b);

32 And to devise [acurious works](#note32a), to work in gold, and in silver, and in brass,

33 And in the cutting of stones, to set them, and in carving of wood, to [amake](#note33a) any manner of cunning work.

34 And he hath put in his heart that he may [ateach](#note34a), both he, and Aholiab, the son of Ahisamach, of the tribe of Dan.

35 Them hath he filled with [awisdom](#note35a) of heart, to [bwork](#note35b) all manner of work, of the engraver, and of the [ccunning workman](#note35c), and of the embroiderer, in blue, and in purple, in scarlet, and in fine linen, and of the weaver, even of them that do any work, and of those that devise cunning work.

Chapter 36

Wise-hearted men are chosen to work on the tabernacle—Moses restrains the people from donating any more material.

1 Then wrought [aBezaleel](#note1a) and Aholiab, and [bevery wise hearted man](#note1b), in whom the Lord put [cwisdom](#note1c) and understanding to know how to work all manner of work [dfor the service of](#note1d) the sanctuary, according to all that the Lord had commanded.

2 And Moses called Bezaleel and Aholiab, and every wise hearted man, in whose [aheart](#note2a) the Lord had put wisdom, even every one whose heart stirred him up to come unto the work to do it:

3 And they received of Moses all the [aoffering](#note3a), which the children of Israel had brought for the work of the service of the sanctuary, to make it withal. And they brought yet unto him [bfree](#note3b) offerings every morning.

4 And all the [awise](#note4a) men, that wrought all the work of the sanctuary, came every man from his work which they made;

5 ¶ And they spake unto Moses, saying, The people [abring](#note5a) much more than enough for the service of the work, which the Lord commanded to make.

6 And Moses gave commandment, and they caused it to be proclaimed throughout the camp, saying, Let neither man nor woman make any more work for the offering of the sanctuary. So the people were restrained from bringing.

7 For the [astuff](#note7a) they had was sufficient for all the work to make it, and too much.

8 ¶ And every wise hearted man among them that wrought the work of the tabernacle [amade](#note8a) ten [bcurtains](#note8b) of fine twined linen, and blue, and purple, and scarlet: with cherubims of cunning work made he them.

9 The length of [aone](#note9a) curtain was twenty and eight cubits, and the breadth of one curtain four cubits: the curtains were all of one size.

10 And he coupled the five curtains one unto another: and the other five curtains he coupled one unto another.

11 And he made loops of blue on the edge of one curtain [afrom](#note11a) the selvedge in the coupling: likewise he made in the uttermost side of another curtain, in the coupling of the second.

12 Fifty loops made he in one curtain, and fifty loops made he in the edge of the curtain which was in the coupling of the second: the loops held one curtain to another.

13 And he made fifty [ataches](#note13a) of gold, and coupled the curtains one unto another with the taches: so it became one tabernacle.

14 ¶ And he made curtains of goats’ hair for the tent over the tabernacle: eleven curtains he made them.

15 The length of one curtain was thirty cubits, and four cubits was the breadth of one curtain: the eleven curtains were of one size.

16 And he coupled five curtains by themselves, and six curtains by themselves.

17 And he made fifty loops upon the uttermost edge of [athe](#note17a) curtain in the coupling, and fifty loops made he upon the edge of the curtain which coupleth the second.

18 And he made fifty taches of brass to couple the tent together, that it might be one.

19 And he made a covering for the tent of rams’ skins dyed red, and a covering of badgers’ skins above that.

20 ¶ And he made [aboards](#note20a) for the tabernacle of [bshittim](#note20b) wood, standing up.

21 The length of a board was ten cubits, and the breadth of a board one cubit and a half.

22 One board had two tenons, [aequally](#note22a) distant one from another: thus did he make for all the boards of the tabernacle.

23 And he made boards for the tabernacle; twenty boards for the south side southward:

24 And forty [asockets](#note24a) of silver he made under the twenty boards; two sockets under one board for his two tenons, and two sockets under another board for his two tenons.

25 And for the other side of the tabernacle, which is toward the north corner, he made twenty boards,

26 And their forty sockets of silver; two sockets under one board, and two sockets under another board.

27 And for the sides of the tabernacle westward he made six boards.

28 And two boards made he for the corners of the tabernacle in the [atwo sides](#note28a).

29 And they were coupled beneath, and coupled together at the head thereof, to one ring: thus he did to both of them in both the corners.

30 And there were eight boards; and their sockets were sixteen sockets of silver, under every board two sockets.

31 ¶ And he made bars of shittim wood; five for the boards of the one side of the tabernacle,

32 And five bars for the boards of the other side of the tabernacle, and five bars for the boards of the tabernacle for the sides westward.

33 And he made the middle bar to [ashoot](#note33a) through the boards from the one end to the other.

34 And he overlaid the boards with gold, and made their rings of gold to be places for the bars, and overlaid the bars with gold.

35 ¶ And he made a [aveil](#note35a) of blue, and purple, and scarlet, and fine twined linen: with cherubims made he it of cunning work.

36 And he made thereunto four pillars of shittim wood, and overlaid them with gold: their hooks were of gold; and he cast for them four sockets of silver.

37 ¶ And he made [aan hanging](#note37a) for the tabernacle door of blue, and purple, and scarlet, and fine twined linen, of needlework;

38 And the five pillars of it with their hooks: and he overlaid their [achapiters](#note38a) and their fillets with gold: but their five sockets were of brass.

Chapter 37

Bezaleel makes the ark, the mercy seat, and the cherubims—He makes the table, the vessels, the candlestick, the incense altar, the holy anointing oil, and the sweet incense.

1 And Bezaleel [amade](#note1a) the [bark](#note1b) of [cshittim](#note1c) wood: two cubits and a half was the length of it, and a cubit and a half the breadth of it, and a cubit and a half the height of it:

2 And he overlaid it with pure gold within and without, and made a [acrown](#note2a) of gold to it round about.

3 And he cast for it four rings of gold, to be set by the four corners of it; even two rings upon the one side of it, and two rings upon the other side of it.

4 And he made staves of shittim wood, and overlaid them with gold.

5 And he put the staves into the rings by the sides of the ark, to bear the ark.

6 ¶ And he made the [amercy seat](#note6a) of pure gold: two cubits and a half was the length thereof, and one cubit and a half the breadth thereof.

7 And he made two [acherubims](#note7a) of gold, beaten out of one piece made he them, on the two ends of the mercy seat;

8 One cherub on the end on this side, and another cherub on the other end on that side: [aout of](#note8a) the mercy seat made he the cherubims on the two ends thereof.

9 And the [acherubims](#note9a) spread out their wings on high, and covered with their wings over the mercy seat, with their faces one to another; even to the mercy seatward were the faces of the cherubims.

10 ¶ And he made the [atable](#note10a) of shittim wood: two cubits was the length thereof, and a cubit the breadth thereof, and a cubit and a half the height thereof:

11 And he overlaid it with pure gold, and made thereunto a crown of gold round about.

12 Also he made thereunto a border of an handbreadth round about; and made a crown of gold for the border thereof round about.

13 And he cast for it four rings of gold, and put the rings upon the four corners that were in the four feet thereof.

14 [aOver against](#note14a) the border were the rings, the places for the staves to bear the table.

15 And he made the staves of shittim wood, and overlaid them with gold, to bear the table.

16 And he made the [avessels](#note16a) which were upon the table, his dishes, and his spoons, and his bowls, and [bhis covers](#note16b) to cover withal, of pure gold.

17 ¶ And he made the [acandlestick](#note17a) of pure gold: of beaten work made he the candlestick; his shaft, and [bhis](#note17b) branch, his bowls, [chis knops](#note17c), and his flowers, were of the same:

18 And six branches going out of the sides thereof; three branches of the candlestick out of the one side thereof, and three branches of the candlestick out of the other side thereof:

19 Three bowls made after the fashion of almonds in one branch, a knop and a flower; and three bowls made like almonds in another branch, a knop and a flower: so throughout the six branches going out of the candlestick.

20 And in the candlestick were four bowls made like almonds, his knops, and his flowers:

21 And a knop under two branches of the same, and a knop under two branches of the same, and a knop under two branches of the same, according to the six branches going out of it.

22 Their knops and their branches were of the same: all of it was one beaten work of pure gold.

23 And he made his seven lamps, and his snuffers, and his snuffdishes, of pure gold.

24 Of a talent of pure gold made he it, and all the vessels thereof.

25 ¶ And he made the incense [aaltar](#note25a) of shittim wood: the length of it was a cubit, and the breadth of it a cubit; it was foursquare; and two cubits was the height of it; the horns thereof were of the same.

26 And he overlaid it with pure gold, both the top of it, and the sides thereof round about, and the horns of it: also he made unto it a crown of gold round about.

27 And he made two rings of gold for it under the crown thereof, by the two corners of it, upon the two sides thereof, to be places for the staves [ato bear it withal](#note27a).

28 And he made the staves of shittim wood, and overlaid them with gold.

29 ¶ And he made the holy anointing oil, and the pure [aincense](#note29a) of sweet spices, according to the work of the [bapothecary](#note29b).

Chapter 38

Bezaleel and others make the altar of burnt offerings and all things pertaining to the tabernacle—Offerings are made by 603,550 men.

1 And he [amade](#note1a) the [baltar](#note1b) of burnt offering of [cshittim](#note1c) wood: five cubits was the length thereof, and five cubits the breadth thereof; it was foursquare; and three cubits the height thereof.

2 And he made the horns thereof on the four corners of it; the horns thereof were of [athe same](#note2a): and he overlaid it with [bbrass](#note2b).

3 And he made all the vessels of the altar, the pots, and the shovels, and the basins, and the fleshhooks, and the firepans: all the vessels thereof made he of brass.

4 And he made for the altar a brasen grate of network under [athe compass](#note4a) thereof beneath unto the midst of it.

5 And he cast four rings for the four ends of the grate of brass, to be places for the staves.

6 And he made the staves of shittim wood, and overlaid them with brass.

7 And he put the staves into the rings on the sides of the altar, to bear it withal; he made the altar hollow with boards.

8 ¶ And he made the laver of brass, and the foot of it of brass, of the [alookingglasses](#note8a) of the women assembling, which assembled at the door of the tabernacle of the congregation.

9 ¶ And he made the court: on the south side southward the hangings of the court were of fine twined linen, an hundred cubits:

10 Their [apillars](#note10a) were twenty, and their brasen [bsockets](#note10b) twenty; the hooks of the pillars and their fillets were of silver.

11 And for the north side the hangings were an hundred cubits, their pillars were twenty, and their sockets of brass twenty; the hooks of the pillars and their fillets of silver.

12 And for the west side were hangings of fifty cubits, their pillars ten, and their sockets ten; the hooks of the pillars and their fillets of silver.

13 And for the east side eastward fifty cubits.

14 The hangings of the one side of the gate were fifteen cubits; their pillars three, and their sockets three.

15 And for the other side of the court gate, on this hand and that hand, were hangings of fifteen cubits; their pillars three, and their sockets three.

16 All the hangings of the court round about were of fine twined [alinen](#note16a).

17 And the sockets for the pillars were of brass; the hooks of the pillars and their fillets of silver; and the overlaying of their [achapiters](#note17a) of silver; and all the [bpillars](#note17b) of the court were filleted with silver.

18 And the [ahanging](#note18a) for the gate of the court was needlework, of blue, and purple, and scarlet, and fine twined linen: and twenty cubits was the length, and the height in the breadth was five cubits, [banswerable](#note18b) to the hangings of the court.

19 And their pillars were four, and their sockets of brass four; their hooks of silver, and the overlaying of their chapiters and their fillets of silver.

20 And all the pins of the tabernacle, and of the court round about, were of brass.

21 ¶ This is the [asum](#note21a) of the [btabernacle](#note21b), even of the [ctabernacle](#note21c) of testimony, as it was counted, according to the commandment of Moses, for the service of the [dLevites](#note21d), by the hand of [eIthamar](#note21e), son to Aaron the priest.

22 And Bezaleel the son of Uri, the son of Hur, of the tribe of Judah, made all that the Lord commanded Moses.

23 And with him was Aholiab, son of Ahisamach, of the tribe of Dan, an engraver, and a cunning workman, and an embroiderer in blue, and in purple, and in scarlet, and fine linen.

24 All the gold that was [aoccupied](#note24a) for the work in all the work of the holy place, even the gold of the [boffering](#note24b), was twenty and nine talents, and seven hundred and thirty shekels, after the shekel of the sanctuary.

25 And the silver of them that were numbered of the congregation was an hundred talents, and a thousand seven hundred and threescore and fifteen shekels, after the shekel of the sanctuary:

26 A bekah for every man, that is, half a shekel, after the [ashekel](#note26a) of the sanctuary, for every one [bthat](#note26b) went to be numbered, from twenty years old and upward, for six hundred thousand and three thousand and five hundred and fifty men.

27 And of the hundred talents of silver were cast the sockets of the sanctuary, and the sockets of the veil; an hundred sockets of the hundred talents, a talent for a socket.

28 And of the thousand seven hundred seventy and five shekels he made hooks for the pillars, and overlaid their chapiters, and filleted them.

29 And the brass of the offering was seventy talents, and two thousand and four hundred shekels.

30 And therewith he made the sockets to the door of the tabernacle of the congregation, and the brasen altar, and the brasen grate for it, and all the vessels of the altar,

31 And the sockets of the court round about, and the sockets of the court gate, and all the pins of the tabernacle, and all the pins of the court round about.

Chapter 39

Holy garments are made for Aaron and the priests—The breastplate is made—The tabernacle of the congregation is finished—Moses blesses the people.

1 And of the blue, and purple, and scarlet, they [amade](#note1a) [bcloths of service](#note1b), to do service in the holy place, and made the holy [cgarments](#note1c) for Aaron; as the Lord commanded Moses.

2 And he made the [aephod](#note2a) of gold, blue, and purple, and scarlet, and fine twined linen.

3 And they did beat the gold into thin plates, and cut it into [awires](#note3a), to work it in the blue, and in the purple, and in the scarlet, and in the fine linen, with [bcunning work](#note3b).

4 They made shoulderpieces for it, to couple it together: by the two edges was it coupled together.

5 And the [acurious girdle](#note5a) of his ephod, that was upon it, was of the same, according to the work thereof; of gold, blue, and purple, and scarlet, and fine twined linen; as the Lord commanded Moses.

6 ¶ And they wrought onyx stones inclosed in [aouches](#note6a) of gold, graven, as signets are graven, with the names of the children of Israel.

7 And he put them on the shoulders of the ephod, that they should be stones for a memorial to the children of Israel; as the Lord commanded Moses.

8 ¶ And he made the breastplate of cunning work, like the work of the ephod; of gold, blue, and purple, and scarlet, and fine twined linen.

9 It was foursquare; they made the breastplate double: a span was the length thereof, and a span the breadth thereof, being doubled.

10 And they set in it four rows of stones: the first row was a [asardius](#note10a), a topaz, and a carbuncle: this was the first row.

11 And the second row, an emerald, a sapphire, and a diamond.

12 And the third row, a [aligure](#note12a), an agate, and an amethyst.

13 And the fourth row, a beryl, an onyx, and a jasper: they were inclosed in ouches of gold in their inclosings.

14 And the stones were according to the names of the children of Israel, twelve, according to their names, like the engravings of a signet, every one with his name, according to the twelve tribes.

15 And they made upon the breastplate chains at the ends, of [awreathen work](#note15a) of pure gold.

16 And they made two ouches of gold, and two gold rings; and put the two rings in the two ends of the breastplate.

17 And they put the two wreathen chains of gold in the two rings on the ends of the breastplate.

18 And the two ends of the two wreathen chains they fastened in the two ouches, and put them on the shoulderpieces of the ephod, before it.

19 And they made two rings of gold, and put them on the two ends of the breastplate, upon the border of it, which was on the side of the ephod inward.

20 And they made two other golden rings, and put them on the two sides of the ephod underneath, toward the forepart of it, over against the other coupling thereof, above the curious girdle of the ephod.

21 And they did bind the breastplate by his rings unto the rings of the ephod with a lace of blue, that it might be above the curious girdle of the ephod, and that the breastplate might not be loosed from the ephod; as the Lord commanded Moses.

22 ¶ And he made the robe of the ephod of woven work, all of blue.

23 And there was an hole in the midst of the robe, as the hole of an [ahabergeon](#note23a), with a band round about the hole, that it should not rend.

24 And they made upon the hems of the robe pomegranates of blue, and purple, and scarlet, and twined linen.

25 And they made bells of pure gold, and put the bells between the pomegranates upon the hem of the robe, round about between the pomegranates;

26 A bell and a pomegranate, a bell and a pomegranate, round about the hem of the robe to minister in; as the Lord commanded Moses.

27 ¶ And they made coats of fine [alinen](#note27a) of woven work for Aaron, and for his sons,

28 And a [amitre](#note28a) of fine linen, and [bgoodly](#note28b) [cbonnets](#note28c) of fine linen, and linen [dbreeches](#note28d) of fine twined linen,

29 And a girdle of fine twined linen, and blue, and purple, and scarlet, of [aneedlework](#note29a); as the Lord commanded Moses.

30 ¶ And they made the plate of the holy crown of pure gold, and wrote upon it a writing, like to the engravings of a signet, [aHoliness](#note30a) to the Lord.

31 And they tied unto it a lace of blue, to fasten it on high upon the mitre; as the Lord commanded Moses.

32 ¶ Thus was all the work of the tabernacle of the tent of the congregation finished: and the children of Israel did according to all that the Lord [acommanded](#note32a) Moses, so did they.

33 ¶ And they brought the [atabernacle](#note33a) unto Moses, the tent, and all [bhis furniture](#note33b), his taches, his boards, his bars, and his pillars, and his sockets,

34 And the covering of rams’ skins dyed red, and the covering of badgers’ skins, and the [aveil of the covering](#note34a),

35 The ark of the testimony, and the staves thereof, and the mercy seat,

36 The table, and all the vessels thereof, and the [ashewbread](#note36a),

37 The pure candlestick, with the lamps thereof, even with the lamps to be set in order, and all the vessels thereof, and the oil for light,

38 And the golden altar, and the anointing oil, and the sweet incense, and the [ahanging](#note38a) for the tabernacle door,

39 The brasen altar, and his grate of brass, his staves, and all his vessels, the laver and [ahis foot](#note39a),

40 The hangings of the court, his pillars, and his sockets, and the hanging for the court gate, his cords, and his pins, and all the vessels of the service of the tabernacle, for the tent of the congregation,

41 The cloths of service to do service in the holy place, and the holy garments for Aaron the priest, and his sons’ garments, to minister in the priest’s office.

42 According to all that the Lord commanded Moses, so the children of Israel made all the work.

43 And Moses did look upon all the work, and, behold, they had done it as the Lord had commanded, even so had they done it: and Moses blessed them.

Chapter 40

The tabernacle is reared—Aaron and his sons are washed and anointed and given an everlasting priesthood—The glory of the Lord fills the tabernacle—A cloud covers the tabernacle by day, and fire rests on it by night.

1 And the Lord spake unto Moses, saying,

2 On the first day of the first [amonth](#note2a) shalt thou set up the [btabernacle](#note2b) of the tent of the [ccongregation](#note2c).

3 And thou shalt put therein the [aark](#note3a) of the testimony, and cover the ark with the [bveil](#note3b).

4 And thou shalt bring in the table, and [aset](#note4a) in order the things that are to be set in order upon it; and thou shalt bring in the candlestick, and light the lamps thereof.

5 And thou shalt set the altar of gold for the incense before the ark of the testimony, and [aput](#note5a) the hanging of the door to the tabernacle.

6 And thou shalt set the altar of the burnt offering before the door of the tabernacle of the tent of the congregation.

7 And thou shalt set the laver between the tent of the congregation and the altar, and shalt put water therein.

8 And thou shalt set up the court round about, and hang up the [ahanging](#note8a) at the court gate.

9 And thou shalt take the anointing oil, and anoint the [atabernacle](#note9a), and all that is therein, and shalt hallow it, and all the vessels thereof: and it shall be holy.

10 And thou shalt anoint the altar of the burnt offering, and all his vessels, and sanctify the altar: and it shall be an altar most holy.

11 And thou shalt anoint the laver and [ahis foot](#note11a), and sanctify it.

12 And thou shalt bring Aaron and his sons unto the door of the [atabernacle of the congregation](#note12a), and wash them with water.

13 And thou shalt put upon Aaron the holy garments, and [aanoint](#note13a) him, and sanctify him; that he may minister unto me in the priest’s office.

14 And thou shalt bring his sons, and clothe them with coats:

15 And thou shalt [aanoint](#note15a) them, as thou didst anoint their father, that they may minister unto me in the [bpriest’s](#note15b) office: for their [canointing](#note15c) shall surely be [dan](#note15d) [eeverlasting](#note15e) [fpriesthood](#note15f) throughout their [ggenerations](#note15g).

16 Thus did Moses: according to all that the Lord commanded him, so did he.

17 ¶ And it came to pass in the first month in the second year, on the first day of the month, that the tabernacle was [areared](#note17a) up.

18 And Moses reared up the tabernacle, and fastened [ahis sockets](#note18a), and set up the boards thereof, and put in the bars thereof, and reared up his pillars.

19 And he spread abroad the tent over the tabernacle, and put the covering of the tent above upon it; as the Lord commanded Moses.

20 ¶ And he took and put the [atestimony](#note20a) into the ark, and set the [bstaves](#note20b) on the ark, and put the mercy seat above upon the ark:

21 And he brought the ark into the tabernacle, and set up the [aveil](#note21a) of the covering, and covered the ark of the testimony; as the Lord commanded Moses.

22 ¶ And he put the table in the tent of the congregation, upon the side of the tabernacle northward, without the veil.

23 And he set the bread in [aorder](#note23a) upon it before the Lord; as the Lord had commanded Moses.

24 ¶ And he put the candlestick in the tent of the congregation, [aover against](#note24a) the table, on the side of the tabernacle southward.

25 And he lighted the [alamps](#note25a) before the Lord; as the Lord commanded Moses.

26 ¶ And he put the golden altar in the tent of the congregation before the veil:

27 And he burnt sweet [aincense](#note27a) thereon; as the Lord commanded Moses.

28 ¶ And he set up the hanging at the door of the tabernacle.

29 And he put the altar of burnt offering by the door of the tabernacle of the tent of the congregation, and offered upon it the burnt offering and the [ameat](#note29a) offering; as the Lord commanded Moses.

30 ¶ And he set the laver between the tent of the congregation and the altar, and put water there, [ato wash](#note30a) withal.

31 And Moses and Aaron and his sons washed their hands and their feet thereat:

32 When they went into the tent of the congregation, and when they came near unto the altar, they washed; as the Lord commanded Moses.

33 And he reared up the court round about the tabernacle and the altar, and set up the hanging of the court gate. So Moses finished the work.

34 ¶ Then a [acloud](#note34a) covered the tent of the congregation, and the [bglory](#note34b) of the Lord [cfilled](#note34c) the [dtabernacle](#note34d).

35 And Moses was not able to enter into the tent of the congregation, because the cloud abode thereon, and the glory of the Lord filled the tabernacle.

36 And when the [acloud](#note36a) was taken up from over the tabernacle, the children of Israel went onward in all their journeys:

37 But if the cloud were not taken up, then they [ajourneyed](#note37a) not till the day that it was taken up.

38 For the [acloud](#note38a) of the Lord was upon the tabernacle by day, and fire was on it by night, in the sight of all the house of Israel, throughout all their journeys.
